Radhakrishnan)Ì¯¿¼Á ¶Î¾Îº¶Ç+ÆÐºÆ §Þ¹Æ¸¼Æ £Á¼Æ¯Í¿, ©¸¯ÆÐ ¥·Æ¶±Æ±·Æ¶¼Æ¹Æ¹¶ÆÎ¶ £¿È¶Æ¶Îº¯Æ¯Ç¯ §+Æ¯à¯ÆÐ ·½È çÞ¯ÈÍ½°¥Þ £Á±¼¯Ç¾±Æ ±´Æ´ ·É¹ÆÚ¹Æ Í¼¼Îµ ºÉ¶Ç¸ ÁÇ¶ºÆ·Î´Ì¹Þ¯È½×° ¥·Æ¶ £Á±¼¯Ç¾±Æ ±´Æ´ºÆ £Á±È»ºÆ¶Ç¸Ç?¥·Æ·Ç´ÆÕ º¯Æ¯Î¿¹Æ ¹Ç×¯Ç¯Æ¯âºÆ ¥·Æ·Ç´ÆÎ´¹Æ ¹Ç×¯Ç¯Æ¯âºÆ£Á±¼¯Ç¾±Æ ±´Æ´ºÆ Ì¯Ç®Õ Á¼¹Æ¹Õ¯È½× ©Þ ç½¹Æ¹´Æ´×°¤¸Ç¾Æ, ¥× ¥¼®ÕÍº ·Î´Ì¹ÞÁ¶Ç¯ ¥¾ÆÎ¾° ¥·Æ¶£Á±¼¯Ç¾±Æ ±´Æ´¶Æ¶È¸Ç¾Æ º¯Æ¯¿Æ Ì¹¼È×ºÆ ¹Ç¶È¹Æ¹Î´¯È½Ç¯¿Æ°Ð½È¹Æ¹Ç¯, ¶ºÈÀÆ º¯Æ¯¿Æ Ì¹¼È×ºÆ ¹Ç¶È¹Æ¹Î´¯È½Ç¼Æ¯¿Æ°£·ÇÁ±È»ºÇ¸ Î¯×¯¿Æ ¥´ºÆÌ¹Þ¯È½¸° ¥Þ »Ç¼ÇÁ×¬ÝÁ¼Æ ¬Ý ¶ºÈÀÎ¸¹Æ ¹Ç¼Æ¶Æ× “¥Á¼Æ Ú” ©Þ ç½È´Æ´Ç¾ÆÍ¹Ç×ºÆ, §´Í¸ £ÁÎ¼¹Æ Ì¹Ç ·ÈÎ¾»¶Æ¶È½ÆÐ¯Æ Ì¯Ç®ÕÌ±Þ £Î´¯Æ¯È½Ç¼Æ¯¿Æ° ¥¹Æ¹»Ç¸ ¬Ý éÀ¾Æ ¶Ç ¥Þ¥Ý¯Æ¯È½×°

Hon. Prime Minister, I would like to bring one incident foryour kind consideration. On the 26th of April, five Tamilyouths were gruesomely murdered and dumped in theAvissawella area. At the All Party Conference we brought upthis matter and the Inspector General of Police told us thatthere will be an impartial investigation and the outcomewill be let known to the nation. To date nothing has happened.

Mr. Mahalingam from Wattala, the father of one of themurdered youths, telephoned me a little while ago. He hasidentified his son’s body, who had been grusesomelymurdered on the 26th of April. He wants to have the funeralon the coming Saturday, the 8th and the body is still at theKalubowila Hospital. He made a request: he asked me totelephone the Avissawella Police and request their assistanceto get this body released as early as possible so that he canhave the furneral at 3.00 p.m. at the Wattala crematorium.There five youths were beheaded. I think, Hon. PrimeMinister, you are well aware of this. I would kindly urge youin this House, in this aughst Assembly, to give assistance toMr. Mahalingam and see that every help is given to him totake his son’s body to Wattala. The Government should bearthe expenses, I urge you, Hon Prime Minister, as a gesture of

2006 °ìÈè 0622752276

goodwill as it always says that it is concerned about all thecitizens of this country. You must do something about it. Iwould kindly urge you to instruct the Officer-In-Charge ofthe Avissawella Police to extend all his assistance to Mr.Mahalingam, who is the father of Mahendra Kumar,commonly known as ‘Sana’, who was gruesomely murdered.Also I would request you to go into this matter and let usknow what has happened. All the five youths were Tamils.They were beheaded. ¥¹Æ¹»Ç¯¶Æ¶Ç £Á±¼¯Ç¾±Æ ±´Æ´ºÆ£Û¾Æ ¥Ý¯ÆÐºÆÍ¹Ç×ºÆ ±ºÆ¹Á+Æ¯¿Æ ¥´ºÆÌ¹Þ¯È½¸° ¥×º´ÆÕº¾Æ¾, ¥·Æ¶ £Á±¼¯Ç¾±Æ ±´Æ´ºÆ £Û¾Æ ¥Ý¯ÆÐºÆÍ¹Ç×¶Ç¼¹¾ Á¼Æ¶Æ¶¯¼Æ¯¿Æ ¯´¶Æ¶¹Æ¹´ÆÝ¯Æ¯È½Ç¼Æ¯¿Æ° ¥·Æ¶¯Æ¯´¶Æ¶¾Æ¯¿ÈÍ¾ ¦Õ¹´Æ´Á¼Æ¯à¯ÆÐºÆ £¼±Ç+Æ¯¶Æ¶È½ÆÐºÆ ±ºÆ¹·Æ¶ºÆ¥Ý¯Æ¯È½× ©ÞºÆ ·Ç+Æ¯¿Æ £½È¯ÈÍ½ÇºÆ° ¤¸Ç¾Æ,£Á¼Æ¯à¯ÆÐ ©¶È¼Ç¯ ©·Æ¶¶ºÇ¸ ·´Á¯ÆÎ¯ÜºÆ©Õ¯Æ¯¹Æ¹´Æ´¶Ç¯¶Æ Ì¶¼È»¾ÆÎ¾° ±ºÆ¹·Æ¶¹Æ¹´Æ´Á¼Æ¯¿Æ£Î´»Ç¿ºÆ ¯Çµ¹Æ¹´Æ´ÇßºÆ £Á¼Æ¯à¯ÆÐ ©¶È¼Ç¯ ·´Á¯ÆÎ¯©Õ¹Æ¹¶Ç¯ ¥¾ÆÎ¾° ¥¹Æ¹Ì»¾Æ¾ÇºÆ ±ºÆ¹Á+Æ¯¿Æ ·´¯ÆÐºÆÍ¹Ç×¥·Æ¶ £Á±¼¯Ç¾±Æ ±´Æ´ºÆ £Á±È»ºÆ¶Ç¸Ç?

The Government has failed to protect its citizens in spiteof having the Emergency Regulations in force. So, what isthe use of this Emergency?

The day before yesterday, the Hon. MahindaSamarasinghe had a press conference and suggested, someguidelines to the police officers and the defence authoritiesto be followed when arresting a person. But in Hatton, I hearone body has been arrested and his father is unable to knowhis whereabouts. Only the day before yesterday theseguidelines were announced and today they are not beingfollowed. We are not able to trece the people who are beingarrested. So, this is the way things are happening. I wouldurge the Hon. Prime Minister to look into these incidentsand see that the police do their duty according to theguidelines given by you. º¯Æ¯¿Æ Õ¶Î¾ Û¸µÈ¼±Ç¼±Æ Ì±»¾Ç¿ÝºÆ Ì¯¿¼Á ¹Ç¼Çàº½ §Þ¹Æ¸ÝºÇ¯È»º¾Æ ¼Á+Æ± £Á¼Æ¯¿Æ ¥Þ ¯ÇÎ¾Í¾ ¥+ÆÐ Í¹ÒºÆÍ¹Ç×Ú¯¿Æ ¥»¯Æ¯¶ÆÎ¶¶Æ ¶Î´Ì±»Æ» ÍÁ®ÕºÆ ©ÞºÆ Ú¯Î¿£ÀÈ¯Æ¯ ÍÁ®ÕºÆ ©ÞºÆ ç½È¸Ç¼Æ° Ú¯¿Æ ¥»¯Æ¯¶ÆÎ¶¶Æ ¶Î´Ì±»ÆÁ¶ÇßºÆ Ú¯Î¿ £ÀÈ¹Æ¹¶ÇßºÆ ¥·Æ¶ ¥¸¹Æ ¼±Æ±ÈÎ¸¯ÆÐ¶Æ¶É¼Æâ ¯®Õ´ ÛÜºÇ ? ¥× ¥¸¹Æ ¼±Æ±ÈÎ¸¯ÆÐ ÌºÍºßºÆ©¼È»[´ÆÕÍº ¶¼, £¶½ÆÐ¼È» ¶É¼ÆÁÇ¯Ç×° ¥Þ ¥·Æ¶È»Ç·ÈÎ¾¹Æ¹ÇÕ ºÇ½È¯Æ Ì¯Ç®Õ ÁÝ¯È½×° ¥Þ Ø{½ÆÞ¯Æ ¯µ¯Æ¯Ç¸¶ºÈÀÆ £¯¶È¯¿Æ ¥·Æ¶È»¯Æ ¯Î¼Î»¹Æ Í¹Ç»Æ±Æ Í±Ý¯È½Ç¼Æ¯¿Æ°¥¶¸Ç¾Æ ª½Æ¹ÕºÆ £Ù¶Ç¹ §µ¼Æ¸Ç¾Æ ¥·Æ¶È» º¯Æ¯¿Æº¸¶ÈÍ¾ÜºÆ ºÇ½Æ½ºÆ ª½Æ¹´ÆÕ ÁÝ¯È½×° £Á¼Æ¯¿Æ ¥·Æ¶È»£¼±Ç+Æ¯¶Æ¶È½ÆÐ £á¶Æ¶ºÆ Ì¯ÇÕ¶Æ× ÁÝ¯È½Ç¼Æ¯¿Æ° ¥¶¸Ç¾Æ¥·Æ¶È»ÇÍÁ Ú¯¿Æ ¥»¯Æ¯¶Æ¶È ºÉ¶Ç¸ ¶Î´Î» ·É¯Æ¯¯ÆçÕÍºÇ©Þ ©®µ¶Æ Í¶ÇÞ¯È½ ¥·Æ¶ Í·¼¶Æ¶ÈÍ¾, º¯Æ¯¿Æ Õ¶Î¾Û¸µÈ ¥+ÆÐ Ú¯¿Æ ¥»¯Æ¯¶ÆÎ¶¶Æ ¶Î´ Ì±»ÆÜºÇÞ Í¯ÇÝÁ×±ºÇ¶Ç¸ ÛÌ¸Õ¹ÆÚ¯ÆÐ ©·Æ¶ ÁÎ¯ßÍº §¶ÁÇ¶ ¬Ý´»ºÇÐºÆ° ·ÇÎ¿ Í¹Ç¼Æ ò®´Ç¾Æ ©¸ÁÇÐºÆ ? ¥Á¼Æ¯¿Æ ¥ÞÍ¹ÇÝ¯ÆÐ §¼ºÈÕ¯È½Ç¼Æ¯¿Æ ; Í¹Ç¼Æ Ì¶ÇÕ¯Æ¯¹Æ¹´ ÍÁ®ÕºÆ ©Þ©®Ö¯È½Ç¼Æ¯¿Æ° Í¹Ç¼ÈÍ¾ ©×âºÆ ·´¯Æ¯¾ÇºÆ ; »ÇÍ¼Ç ¬ÝÁ¼ÆÌÁ¾ÆÁÇ¼Æ ; »ÇÍ¼Ç ¬ÝÁ¼Æ Í¶Ç½Æ¹Ç¼Æ° ¥Î¶ Ûç´ÆÍ» Ì±Ç¾ÆÁ×¯´ºÆ° £¹Æ¹»Ç¸ ¬Ý éÀ¾Æ ¥Ý¯ÆÐºÆÍ¹Ç× ©¶½Æ¯Ç¯¹Æ Í¹ÇÎ¼¹Æ¹½Æ½È±Æ ±È·Æ¶È¯Æ¯ ÍÁ®ÕºÆ? ©¶½Æ¯Ç¯¹Æ Í¹ÇÎ¼±Æ Ì±»ÆÁ¶½ÆÐ©¶Æ¶¸È¯Æ¯ ÍÁ®ÕºÆ ? ©¸ÍÁ, £Î¶ Õ¶Æ× ±ºÇ¶Ç¸¶ÆÎ¶¯ÆÌ¯Ç®Õ ÁÝÁ¶½Æ¯Ç¸ Û»½Æ±ÈÍ¾ ¦Õ¹´ ÍÁ®ÕºÆ° £¼±Ç+Æ¯ºÆ±ºÇ¶Ç¸ ÛÌ¸Õ¹ÆÎ¹ Í·Ç¯Æ¯È» ¹»µ¶Æ¶È¾Æ ÍÁ¯ºÇ¯±Æ Ì±¾Æ¾

ªÇæ ÇÉêÏà Í¨ù ÄÍºå(ºÇ®ÚºÈÐ ¼Á[¹Æ Ä¯Æ¯ÉºÆ)(The Hon. Rauff Hakeem)

“Bismullahir Rahmanir Raheem’’

Mr. Presiding Member, before I deal with the EmergencyDebate on which the vote is to be taken at the end of theday, since the Hon. deputy Minister of Justice is here, Ithought I will clarify briefly the SLMC’s position on theEighteenth Amendment. I do not know whether you are

2006 °ìÈè 0622792280

taking the vote on the Eighteenth Amendment today. -[Interruption] Anyway, whatever it may be, it is incumbenton the SLMC to clarify its position.

An impression has been created that the SLMC was theparty blocking the passage of this Bill infact the SLMC’sposition was that since the powers of the court of Appealare to be taken to the provinces, the working of the Courtof Appeal in the provinces will enable litigants in thoseareas to transact matters regarding their litigation in thosecourts. We expected certain other jurisdictions, originaljurisdiction vested in the Supreme Court also to be broughtto the Court of Appeal level. But the Hon. Minister of Justicepointed out that this cluster of subjects could be dealt within a separate legislation and that it was not possible for themto concede those amendments. But however, at the last PartyLeaders’ Meeting when the Chief Government Whipinquired from me as to whether we are still keen about theposition that we have taken in the past, I indicated to himthat we do not want to stand in the way of the passage ofthis Bill since the lawyers from Hulftsdorp, various judgesand everybody else appear to think that the Bill needs togo through if cases are to be expedited and that it will alsoenable about 11 more Court of Appeal Judges to beappointed. So in deference to that request we conceded thatwe will support this Bill. So the SLMC will, if the Bill istaken up today, give its wholehearted support.

In the meantime, it is very unfortunate that the mainOpposition has taken up a position not to support the Billtoday and has tied it up with the issue concerning theConstitutional Council. But we expect that some kind ofdiscussion should take place between the two major partiesand this matter be resolved, so that we can give effect tothe Eighteenth Amendment to enable the Court of Appealto function in the Provinces.

We only have one particular concern and that is thefunctioning of the Court of Appeal in the North EastProvince. The purpose of the Amendment is to make it easierfor litigants to transact their business. As it is they have tocome to Colombo to pursue their cases in the Court ofAppeal. Now if the sitting of the Court of Appeal is to bein Trincomalee for people in Ampara and various otherplaces it might make it more difficult. - [Interruption.]

Reforms and Deputy Minister of Constitutional Affairs andNational Integration)It will not happen that way because after 11 more judgesare appointed we will not have it in Trincomalee only.The President of the Court of Appeal will get the judges

to go on circuit various places in the North East Province,not only to Trincomalee on circuit like what the formerCommissioners of Assize did.

“Mahinda invites LTTE to help evolve a peaceful solution”

NEW DELHI, July 4: President Mahinda Rajapakse, has said hewants the Liberation Tigers of Tamil Eelam (LTTE) to activelyparticipate in the efforts to evolve a lasting peaceful solution to theisland’s festering ethnic problem.In an interview to Indian television news channel NDTV broadcasttoday, he said he wants to submit a set of draft proposals for discussionwith the Tigers. The tigers should consider them, respond to them andcome up with their own suggestions and amendments.

ïÂåïÍåÄ ïÍå¿ Àò¨åÊÆ¨à. It further states, I quote:

“The idea is to evolve a solution that will be acceptable to allcommunities inhabiting the island.

Rajapakse pointed out that he does not want to put forth any take-it-or-leave-it kind of proposals and force the Tigers to accept them.”

¦ºëÄå ÈæÍæÌàºø ¾æÍæ, ï¨å¾à´ ÂÈ ¨Ç¾ ïÆåà°¾å ï¼¾à¾.

“He does not want to push them into a corner or make things difficultfor them either.

The President said both LTTE Chief velupillai Prabhakaran and heare Sri Lankans. ‘So, we can sit and discuss this. I am saying to them:Come, discuss and tell us what you want. What I want is for him(Prabhakaran) to come and participate in the whole process.’

Such deliberations can help the government put together ideas andproposals and produce a solution that is acceptable to all Sri Lankans.”

ï¨ ¢ºåÄºàÄ Éæ¼ªºà Àò¨åÊÆ¨à.
